0                                   7143              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                    7144              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7145              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7146              Ÿ  DBLINE - DEBUG LINE                                                Ÿ
                                    7147              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7148              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                    7149              Ÿ       CPEXLINE - EXEC LINE NUMBER                                   Ÿ
                                    7150              Ÿ       CP#XSET - EXEC FILE SET NUMBER                                Ÿ
                                    7151              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7152              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE IS CALLED TO HANDLE ALL DEBUGING TRAPS.  IT           Ÿ
                                    7153              Ÿ  IS SOMEWHAT TRICKY IN THAT EVERYTHING MUST BE HANDLED IN           Ÿ
                                    7154              Ÿ  PROPER ORDER. SOME GENERAL EXPLANATION FOLLOWS...                  Ÿ
                                    7155              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7156              Ÿ  NORMAL TRAP FLAGS:                                                 Ÿ
                                    7157              Ÿ    NEXT FLAG - STOP BEFORE NEXT COMMAND EXECUTION                   Ÿ
                                    7158              Ÿ    STOP FLAG - STOP BEFORE EXECUTING THIS COMMAND                   Ÿ
                                    7159              Ÿ    STOPPED FLAG - WE ARE AT A STOP                                  Ÿ
                                    7160              Ÿ  AT EACH EXEC COMMAND EXECUTION THESE FLAGS ARE CHECKED AND         Ÿ
                                    7161              Ÿ  PROCESSED.  ORDER IN PROCESSING                                    Ÿ
                                    7162              Ÿ  THESE FLAGS IS IMPORTANT... IF WE ARE 'STOPPED', WE DO NOT         Ÿ
                                    7163              Ÿ  PROCESS A 'STOP' FLAG,, AS IT HAS ALREADY BEEN PROCESSED AND       Ÿ
                                    7164              Ÿ  WE HAVE 'STOPPED', AND SO WE DO NOT STOP AGAIN.  THESE THREE       Ÿ
                                    7165              Ÿ  FLAGS ROTATE AROUND AS FOLLOWS:                                    Ÿ
                                    7166              Ÿ       NEXT -> STOP -> STOPPED...                                    Ÿ
                                    7167              Ÿ  WE PROCESS THE FOLLOWING CASES:                                    Ÿ
                                    7168              Ÿ       NEXT,                                                         Ÿ
                                    7169              Ÿ       STOP,                                                         Ÿ
                                    7170              Ÿ       STOPPED,                  (IGNORE STOP FLAG IF SET)           Ÿ
                                    7171              Ÿ       NEXT AND STOPPED.                                             Ÿ
                                    7172              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7173              Ÿ  IMMEDIATE STOP FLAGS:                                              Ÿ
                                    7174              Ÿ  A SIMILAR MECHANISM IS USED FOR STOPPING BEFORE A RETURN           Ÿ
                                    7175              Ÿ  COMMAND... THIS MECHANISM IS KNOWN AS AN IMMEDIATE STOP.           Ÿ
                                    7176              Ÿ  IT USES THE FOLLOWING 3 FLAGS:                                     Ÿ
                                    7177              Ÿ       ISTOP  -> ISTOPPED  -> IDONE                                  Ÿ
                                    7178              Ÿ  THE IDONE FLAG IS NEEDED SO THAT THE COMMAND CAN CHECK IF          Ÿ
                                    7179              Ÿ  IT HAS ALREADY BEEN STOPPED.  CURRENTLY THIS SET OF FLAGS IS       Ÿ
                                    7180              Ÿ  IS ONLY USED TO STOP BEFORE AN 'XRETURN' OR 'RETURN' COMMAND       Ÿ
                                    7181              Ÿ  IS EXECUTED.  THIS TYPE OF STOP OVERRIDES THE OTHER STOP FLAGS     Ÿ
                                    7182              Ÿ  AS IT IS IMMEDIATELY TAKEN.                                        Ÿ
                                    7183              Ÿ  WE PROCESS THE FOLLOWING CASES:                                    Ÿ
                                    7184              Ÿ       ISTOP,    (WE CLEAR ANY REGULAR NEXT, STOP, STOPPED FLAGS)    Ÿ
                                    7185              Ÿ       ISTOPPED                                                      Ÿ
                                    7186              Ÿ       NEXT AND ISTOPPED                                             Ÿ
                                    7187              Ÿ       IDONE                                                         Ÿ
                                    7188              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    7189              Ÿ  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINES SET THESE FLAGS EXTERNAL TO THIS ROUTINE:   Ÿ
                                    7190              Ÿ       NEXT - 'DEBUG NEXT' TYPED      (ONLY ALLOWED AT TRAP BREAK)   Ÿ
                                    7191              Ÿ       STOP - 'LINE NUMBER TRAP' HIT  (SET HERE)                     Ÿ
                                    7192              Ÿ       STOP - 'PROC NAME TRAP' HIT    (IN XCALL,PCALL)               Ÿ
                                    7193              Ÿ       ISTOP - 'RETURN TRAP' HIT      (IN XRETURN, RETURN)           Ÿ
                                    7194              Ÿ  THE REMAINING FLAGS ARE STATE FLAGS AND ARE PROCESSED CAREFULLY    Ÿ
                                    7195              Ÿ  BELOW.                                                             Ÿ
                                    7196              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
